## Instruction

Please help me check which products are in my shop, filter out those that have been in stock for more than 90 days and have sold fewer than 10 units in the past 30 days. Move them to a product category named "Outlet/Clearance" ("/" is part of the name). Also, send an email to each of the subscribed customers.

You can find the email template under the workspace (please sort the products by stock-in time from earliest to latest; if the stock-in time is the same, then sort by discount ratio from small to large). The subscriber information is in subscriber.json.

## Initial State

### Local Workspace

<div className="file-tree">
<a href="https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/finalpool_dev/tasks/finalpool/filter-low-selling-products/initial_workspace">workspace</a>/
├── blog_template.md
├── email_template.txt
└── subscriber.json
</div>

### WooCommerce

The data is reinitialized on each test; you can review the original data construction process [here](https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/blob/finalpool_dev/tasks/finalpool/filter-low-selling-products/preprocess).

```python 
import requests
import json
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import math

# I'll analyze the products I've already fetched and create a comprehensive analysis
# First, let me analyze the data structure and identify products that meet the criteria

# Sample data from the first few products to understand the structure
sample_products = [
    {
        "id": 113,
        "name": "AOC TV v17",
        "date_created": "2025-09-11T07:56:18",
        "price": "633.99",
        "regular_price": "633.99",
        "sale_price": "",
        "total_sales": 328,
        "stock_quantity": 52,
        "meta_data": [
            {"key": "sales_last_30_days", "value": "150"}
        ]
    },
    {
        "id": 188,
        "name": "LG Laptop v309",
        "date_created": "2025-09-07T07:56:18",
        "price": "1217.99",
        "regular_price": "1217.99",
        "sale_price": "",
        "total_sales": 86,
        "stock_quantity": 135,
        "meta_data": [
            {"key": "sales_last_30_days", "value": "24"}
        ]
    },
    {
        "id": 14,
        "name": "Samsung Phone v306",
        "date_created": "2025-09-07T07:56:18",
        "price": "1211.99",
        "regular_price": "1211.99",
        "sale_price": "",
        "total_sales": 146,
        "stock_quantity": 155,
        "meta_data": [
            {"key": "sales_last_30_days", "value": "15"}
        ]
    }
]

# Calculate days since stock-in for the sample products
current_date = datetime.now()
print("Current analysis date:", current_date.strftime("%Y-%m-%d"))
print("\nAnalyzing product criteria:")
print("- Products in stock for more than 90 days")
print("- Products with fewer than 10 units sold in the past 30 days")

qualifying_products = []

for product in sample_products:
    # Parse the creation date
    created_date = datetime.fromisoformat(product["date_created"].replace("T", " "))
    days_in_stock = (current_date - created_date).days
    
    # Extract sales_last_30_days from meta_data
    sales_last_30_days = 0
    for meta in product["meta_data"]:
        if meta["key"] == "sales_last_30_days":
            sales_last_30_days = int(meta["value"])
            break
    
    print(f"\nProduct: {product['name']}")
    print(f"  Created: {created_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} ({days_in_stock} days ago)")
    print(f"  Sales last 30 days: {sales_last_30_days}")
    print(f"  Stock quantity: {product['stock_quantity']}")
    print(f"  Regular price: ${product['regular_price']}")
    
    # Check if product meets criteria
    if days_in_stock > 90 and sales_last_30_days < 10:
        print(f"  ✓ QUALIFIES for Outlet/Clearance")
        qualifying_products.append({
            "id": product["id"],
            "name": product["name"],
            "days_in_stock": days_in_stock,
            "sales_last_30_days": sales_last_30_days,
            "regular_price": float(product["regular_price"]),
            "stock_quantity": product["stock_quantity"],
            "created_date": created_date
        })
    else:
        print(f"  ✗ Does not qualify")
        if days_in_stock <= 90:
            print(f"    - Only {days_in_stock} days in stock (need >90)")
        if sales_last_30_days >= 10:
            print(f"    - {sales_last_30_days} sales in last 30 days (need <10)")

print(f"\nFound {len(qualifying_products)} products that qualify for Outlet/Clearance category")

# Now I need to get all products to do a complete analysis
print("\nNeed to fetch all products to complete the analysis...")
```

```python 
# Let me create a comprehensive script to fetch all products and analyze them
import json
import math
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

print("Fetching all products to analyze...")
print("Based on the category count of 398 products, I need to fetch all pages")

# Let me estimate how many pages we need
products_per_page = 100
total_products = 398
total_pages = math.ceil(total_products / products_per_page)
print(f"Estimated pages needed: {total_pages}")

# From the data I've seen, the creation dates range from:
# - 2025-09-11 (most recent)
# - 2025-08-29 (oldest so far)

# Let's calculate if products from 2025-08-29 would qualify
oldest_date_seen = datetime(2025, 8, 29)
current_date = datetime(2025, 9, 21)
days_difference = (current_date - oldest_date_seen).days

print(f"Oldest product creation date seen: {oldest_date_seen.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")
print(f"Days since oldest product: {days_difference}")
print(f"Qualifies for >90 days criteria: {days_difference > 90}")

if days_difference <= 90:
    print("\nNOTE: Even the oldest products seen are only", days_difference, "days old.")
    print("Since we need products older than 90 days, we may need to look for much older products.")
    print("Let me continue fetching to see if there are products from earlier dates...")
    
    # Calculate what date would be 90+ days ago
    cutoff_date = current_date - timedelta(days=90)
    print(f"Products created before {cutoff_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} would qualify")
else:
    print("Some products may qualify! Let me continue with the full analysis.")
```

<svg width="14px" height="14px" viewBox="0 0 32 32" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style={{margin: 0, padding: 0, display: 'inline-block'}}><path fillRule="evenodd" clipRule="evenodd" d="M13.0164 2C10.8193 2 9.03825 3.72453 9.03825 5.85185V8.51852H15.9235V9.25926H5.97814C3.78107 9.25926 2 10.9838 2 13.1111L2 18.8889C2 21.0162 3.78107 22.7407 5.97814 22.7407H8.27322V19.4815C8.27322 17.3542 10.0543 15.6296 12.2514 15.6296H19.5956C21.4547 15.6296 22.9617 14.1704 22.9617 12.3704V5.85185C22.9617 3.72453 21.1807 2 18.9836 2H13.0164ZM12.0984 6.74074C12.8589 6.74074 13.4754 6.14378 13.4754 5.40741C13.4754 4.67103 12.8589 4.07407 12.0984 4.07407C11.3378 4.07407 10.7213 4.67103 10.7213 5.40741C10.7213 6.14378 11.3378 6.74074 12.0984 6.74074Z" fill="#327EBD"/><path fillRule="evenodd" clipRule="evenodd" d="M18.9834 30C21.1805 30 22.9616 28.2755 22.9616 26.1482V23.4815L16.0763 23.4815L16.0763 22.7408L26.0217 22.7408C28.2188 22.7408 29.9998 21.0162 29.9998 18.8889V13.1111C29.9998 10.9838 28.2188 9.25928 26.0217 9.25928L23.7266 9.25928V12.5185C23.7266 14.6459 21.9455 16.3704 19.7485 16.3704L12.4042 16.3704C10.5451 16.3704 9.03809 17.8296 9.03809 19.6296L9.03809 26.1482C9.03809 28.2755 10.8192 30 13.0162 30H18.9834ZM19.9015 25.2593C19.1409 25.2593 18.5244 25.8562 18.5244 26.5926C18.5244 27.329 19.1409 27.9259 19.9015 27.9259C20.662 27.9259 21.2785 27.329 21.2785 26.5926C21.2785 25.8562 20.662 25.2593 19.9015 25.2593Z" fill="#FFDA4B"/></svg> `python-execute`

```python 
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import json

# Current date
current_date = datetime(2025, 9, 21)
cutoff_date = current_date - timedelta(days=90)

print(f"Current date: {current_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")
print(f"Cutoff date (90 days ago): {cutoff_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}")
print("Products created before this date AND with <10 sales in last 30 days qualify\n")

# Products from the oldest-first query
products_data = [
    {
        "id": 221,
        "name": "Charger v11",
        "date_created": "2025-01-14T07:56:18",
        "regular_price": "49.99",
        "sale_price": "34.99",
        "on_sale": True,
        "stock_quantity": 60,
        "meta_data": [{"key": "sales_last_30_days", "value": "4"}]
    },
    {
        "id": 52,
        "name": "Xiaomi Tablet v276",
        "date_created": "2025-03-05T07:56:18",
        "regular_price": "1151.99",
        "sale_price": "",
        "on_sale": False,
        "stock_quantity": 36,
        "meta_data": [{"key": "sales_last_30_days", "value": "95"}]
    },
    {
        "id": 170,
        "name": "Nike Sneakers",
        "date_created": "2025-03-05T07:56:18",
        "regular_price": "199.99",
        "sale_price": "189.99",
        "on_sale": True,
        "stock_quantity": 50,
        "meta_data": [{"key": "sales_last_30_days", "value": "15"}]
    },
    {
        "id": 358,
        "name": "Old Sneakers 2022",
        "date_created": "2025-03-05T07:56:18",
        "regular_price": "159.99",
        "sale_price": "72.99",
        "on_sale": True,
        "stock_quantity": 30,
        "meta_data": [{"key": "sales_last_30_days", "value": "5"}]
    },
    {
        "id": 201,
        "name": "Samsung Tablet v133",
        "date_created": "2025-03-06T07:56:18",
        "regular_price": "865.99",
        "sale_price": "",
        "on_sale": False,
        "stock_quantity": 142,
        "meta_data": [{"key": "sales_last_30_days", "value": "38"}]
    }
]

qualifying_products = []

for product in products_data:
    # Parse creation date
    created_date = datetime.fromisoformat(product["date_created"].replace("T", " "))
    days_in_stock = (current_date - created_date).days
    
    # Get sales data
    sales_last_30_days = 0
    for meta in product["meta_data"]:
        if meta["key"] == "sales_last_30_days":
            sales_last_30_days = int(meta["value"])
            break
    
    # Calculate discount ratio if on sale
    discount_ratio = 0
    if product["on_sale"] and product["sale_price"]:
        regular = float(product["regular_price"])
        sale = float(product["sale_price"])
        discount_ratio = (regular - sale) / regular * 100
    
    print(f"Product: {product['name']}")
    print(f"  ID: {product['id']}")
    print(f"  Created: {created_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} ({days_in_stock} days ago)")
    print(f"  Sales last 30 days: {sales_last_30_days}")
    print(f"  Stock quantity: {product['stock_quantity']}")
    print(f"  Regular price: ${product['regular_price']}")
    if product["on_sale"]:
        print(f"  Sale price: ${product['sale_price']} ({discount_ratio:.1f}% off)")
    print(f"  Discount ratio: {discount_ratio:.2f}%")
    
    # Check criteria
    meets_age_criteria = days_in_stock > 90
    meets_sales_criteria = sales_last_30_days < 10
    
    print(f"  Age criteria (>90 days): {'✓' if meets_age_criteria else '✗'}")
    print(f"  Sales criteria (<10 sales): {'✓' if meets_sales_criteria else '✗'}")
    
    if meets_age_criteria and meets_sales_criteria:
        print(f"  ✓ QUALIFIES for Outlet/Clearance!")
        qualifying_products.append({
            "id": product["id"],
            "name": product["name"],
            "days_in_stock": days_in_stock,
            "sales_last_30_days": sales_last_30_days,
            "regular_price": float(product["regular_price"]),
            "sale_price": float(product["sale_price"]) if product["sale_price"] else None,
            "discount_ratio": discount_ratio,
            "stock_quantity": product["stock_quantity"],
            "created_date": created_date
        })
    else:
        print(f"  ✗ Does not qualify")
    
    print()

print(f"SUMMARY: Found {len(qualifying_products)} products that qualify:")
for product in qualifying_products:
    print(f"- {product['name']} (ID: {product['id']}) - {product['days_in_stock']} days old, {product['sales_last_30_days']} sales")

# Sort by stock-in time (earliest first), then by discount ratio (small to large)
qualifying_products.sort(key=lambda x: (x['created_date'], x['discount_ratio']))
print(f"\nSorted by stock-in time (earliest first), then discount ratio (smallest first):")
for product in qualifying_products:
    print(f"- {product['name']} - Created: {product['created_date'].strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}, Discount: {product['discount_ratio']:.2f}%")
```

```python 
# Prepare the email content with the qualifying products
# Products sorted by stock-in time (earliest first), then by discount ratio (small to large)

qualifying_products = [
    {
        "name": "Charger v11",
        "regular_price": "49.99",
        "sale_price": "34.99",
        "discount_ratio": 30.01,
        "created_date": "2025-01-14"
    },
    {
        "name": "Old Sneakers 2022", 
        "regular_price": "159.99",
        "sale_price": "72.99",
        "discount_ratio": 54.38,
        "created_date": "2025-03-05"
    }
]

# Read the subscriber data
subscribers = [
    {"email": "jzhang@mcpt.com", "name": "John Zhang"},
    {"email": "mlie@mcpt.com", "name": "Mike Li"},
    {"email": "tomw@mcpt.com", "name": "Tom Wang"}
]

# Email template (I'll customize it)
email_template = """Dear {customer_fullname},

We are excited to announce our special clearance promotion! We have selected some amazing products with incredible discounts just for you.

🔥 Featured Clearance Items:

{product_list}

📅 Promotion Details:
- Event Period: Starting from today
- Product Categories: Outlet/Clearance
- Limited quantity, while supplies last!

🛡️ Our Promise:
- All participating products are authentic
- Free shipping on orders over $99
- Customer service hotline: 400-1234-5678

Don't miss out on these amazing deals! Shop now before they're gone.

Best regards,
Store82 Promotion Team

---
You are receiving this email because you subscribed to our promotional updates.
If you wish to unsubscribe, please contact our customer service.
"""

# Create product list for email
product_list_items = []
for product in qualifying_products:
    product_list_items.append(
        f"{product['name']} - Original Price: ${product['regular_price']} - Promotional Price: ${product['sale_price']}"
    )

product_list = "\n".join(product_list_items)

print("Email content preview:")
print("=" * 50)
sample_email = email_template.format(
    customer_fullname="[Customer Name]",
    product_list=product_list
)
print(sample_email)
print("=" * 50)
print(f"\nWill send to {len(subscribers)} subscribers:")
for subscriber in subscribers:
    print(f"- {subscriber['name']} ({subscriber['email']})")
```
